# All Items

From Project Diablo 2

[Jump to navigation](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/All_Items#mw-head) [Jump to search](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/All_Items#searchInput)

Below is a compilation of all "named" items - unique/set/runeword items and some others, whose affixes are all explicitly determined rather than generated randomly. [Crafted](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Crafting "Crafting") items also have some predetermined affixes, but are not included here.

Other item compilation lists:

- [All Unique Weapons](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/All_Unique_Weapons "All Unique Weapons")
- [All Unique Non-Weapons](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/All_Unique_Non-Weapons "All Unique Non-Weapons")
- [All Set Items](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/All_Set_Items "All Set Items")
- [All Runewords](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/All_Runewords "All Runewords")
- [New Equipment](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/New_Equipment "New Equipment")

# Axes

## Unique Axes

All two-handed axes now gain bonus damage equal to 110% strength instead of 100% strength.

In addition to the changes listed here, all melee weapons also gain Melee Attacks Deal Splash Damage.

Ethereal weapons gain a x1.25 damage bonus instead of a x1.5 damage bonus.

Also see [Throwing Axes](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Throwing "Throwing").

### Normal One-Handed Axes

#### The Gnasher

[![](https://static.wikitide.net/projectdiablo2wiki/c/c3/The_Gnasher.png)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/File:The_Gnasher.png)

**Hand Axe**

- **Base Damage:** 3 to 6

- **Base Durability:** 56 (was 28)

- **Base Speed Modifier:** 0

- **Base Melee Range:** 2 (was 0)

- **Base Maximum Sockets:** 2 (3 for upgraded versions)


**One-Hand Damage:** 4 to \[8-9\], Avg 6-6.5 (was \[4-5\] to \[9-10\], Avg 6.5-7.5)

**Required Level:** 5

| Before | After |
| --- | --- |
| +\[60-70\]% Enhanced Damage | +\[40-50\]% Enhanced Damage |
| 20% Chance of Crushing Blow | 20% Chance of Crushing Blow |
| 50% Chance of Open Wounds | 50% Chance of Open Wounds |
|  | +2 Open Wounds Damage per Second |
| +8 to Strength | +8 to Strength |

### Exceptional Two-Handed Axes

#### Warlord's Trust

- **Base Durability:** 60 (was 30)

# Maces

## Unique Maces

In addition to the changes listed here, all melee weapons also gain Melee Attacks Deal Splash Damage.

Ethereal weapons gain a x1.25 damage bonus instead of a x1.5 damage bonus.

## Special Maces

#### Wirt's Leg

[![](https://static.wikitide.net/projectdiablo2wiki/c/c0/Wirt%27s_Leg.png)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/File:Wirt%27s_Leg.png)

**One-Hand Damage:** 2 to 8, Avg 5

**Durability:** 66

**Speed Modifier:** -10

**Melee Range:** 1

**Maximum Sockets:** 3

**Required Level:** None

| Before | After |
| --- | --- |
| +50% Damage to Undead | +50% Damage to Undead |

This is a regular item that can be used to open the [Secret Cow Level](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Recipes#Portals "Recipes"). It can also be [imbued](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Recipes#Imbue "Recipes"), turned into a [magic item](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Recipes#Equipment_Creation_Recipes "Recipes") to [craft](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Crafting "Crafting") with, or used as a [runeword](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons "RWWeapons") base like other regular items. It is considered a club, so can now get Druid pointmods/staffmods like other clubs.

# Swords

## Unique Swords

All one-handed swords now gain bonus damage equal to 75% strength & 75% dexterity instead of 100% strength.

All two-handed swords now gain bonus damage equal to 110% strength instead of 100% strength.

In addition to the changes listed here, all melee weapons also gain Melee Attacks Deal Splash Damage.

Ethereal weapons gain a x1.25 damage bonus instead of a x1.5 damage bonus.

# Daggers

## Unique Daggers

In addition to the changes listed here, all melee weapons also gain Melee Attacks Deal Splash Damage.

Ethereal weapons gain a x1.25 damage bonus instead of a x1.5 damage bonus.

Also see [Throwing Daggers](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Throwing "Throwing").

### Normal Daggers

#### Gull

[![](https://static.wikitide.net/projectdiablo2wiki/a/aa/Dagger_D2.png)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/File:Dagger_D2.png)

**Dagger**

- **Base Damage:** 1 to 4

- **Base Durability:** 32 (was 16)

- **Base Speed Modifier:** -20

# Throwing Weapons

## Unique Throwing Weapons

Throwing weapons now have unlimited quantity.

In addition to the changes listed here, all melee weapons also gain Melee Attacks Deal Splash Damage.

Ethereal weapons gain a x1.25 damage bonus instead of a x1.5 damage bonus.

See [Class Weapons](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Class_Weapons#Javelins "Class Weapons") for unique Amazon Javelins.

## Special Throwing Weapons

- Throwing potions now reduce enemy resistances
- New versions of throwing potions are now available for the cold and lightning elements

### Low Throwing Potions

#### Fulminating Potion

[![](https://static.wikitide.net/projectdiablo2wiki/8/80/Fulminating_Potion.png)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/File:Fulminating_Potion.png)

**Throw Damage:** 5 to 15 (fire)

**Enemy Fire Resistances:**-3%

**Required Level:** None

#### Strangling Gas Potion

[![](https://static.wikitide.net/projectdiablo2wiki/f/fd/Strangling_Gas_Potion.png)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/File:Strangling_Gas_Potion.png)

**Throw Damage:** 19 over 3 seconds (poison)

**Enemy Poison Resistances:**-3%

**Required Level:** 6

#### Chilling Potion

[![](https://static.wikitide.net/projectdiablo2wiki/b/bf/Chilling_Potion.png)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/File:Chilling_Potion.png)

**Throw Damage:** 3 to 6 (cold)

**Enemy Cold Resistances:** -3%

**Required Level:** None

#### Charged Potion

[![](https://static.wikitide.net/projectdiablo2wiki/c/c3/Charged_Potion.png)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/File:Charged_Potion.png)

**Throw Damage:** 1 to 14 (lightning)

**Enemy Lightning Resistances:** -3%

**Required Level:** 6

# Spears

## Unique Spears

All non-class spears now gain bonus damage equal to 75% strength & 75% dexterity instead of 100% strength.

In addition to the changes listed here, all melee weapons also gain Melee Attacks Deal Splash Damage.

Ethereal weapons gain a x1.25 damage bonus instead of a x1.5 damage bonus.

See [Class Weapons](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Class_Weapons#Spears "Class Weapons") for unique Amazon Spears. Also see [Throwing Spears (Javelins)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Throwing#Elite_Javelins "Throwing").

# Polearms

## Unique Polearms

All polearms now gain bonus damage equal to 75% strength & 75% dexterity instead of 100% strength.

In addition to the changes listed here, all melee weapons also gain Melee Attacks Deal Splash Damage.

Ethereal weapons gain a x1.25 damage bonus instead of a x1.5 damage bonus.

# Bows

## Unique Bows

All bows now gain bonus damage equal to 50% dexterity instead of 100% dexterity.

See [Class Weapons](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Class_Weapons#Bows "Class Weapons") for unique Amazon Bows.

# Staves

## Unique Staves

All staves now gain bonus damage equal to 110% strength instead of 100% strength.

In addition to the changes listed here, all melee weapons also gain Melee Attacks Deal Splash Damage.

Ethereal weapons gain a x1.25 damage bonus instead of a x1.5 damage bonus.

### Normal Staves

## Special Staves

#### Staff of Kings

[![](https://static.wikitide.net/projectdiablo2wiki/0/09/Staff_of_Kings.png)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/File:Staff_of_Kings.png)

| --- | --- |
| +50% Increased Attack Speed | +50% Increased Attack Speed |

# Class Weapons

## Unique Class Weapons

In addition to the changes listed here, all melee weapons also gain Melee Attacks Deal Splash Damage.

Ethereal weapons gain a x1.25 damage bonus instead of a x1.5 damage bonus.

### Amazon

#### Bows

All bows now gain bonus damage equal to 50% dexterity instead of 100% dexterity.

##### Lycander's Aim

[![](https://static.wikitide.net/projectdiablo2wiki/7/7a/Reflex_Bow.png)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/File:Reflex_Bow.png)

- **Base Speed Modifier:** 10


**Two-Hand Damage:**\[96-107\] to \[222-248\], Avg 159-177.5 (was \[72-82\] to \[152-173\], Avg 112-127.5)

**Required Strength:** 73

**Required Dexterity:** 110

**Required Level:** 42

| Before | After |
| --- | --- |
| +2 to Bow and Crossbow Skills (Amazon Only) | +2 to Bow and Crossbow Skills (Amazon Only) |
| +2 to Amazon Skills | +2 to Amazon Skills |
| +20% Increased Attack Speed | +20% Increased Attack Speed |
| +\[150-200\]% Enhanced Damage | +\[225-275\]% Enhanced Damage |
| Adds 25-50 Damage | Adds 25-50 Damage |
|  | -50% Target Defense |
| \[5-8\]% Mana Stolen per Hit | \[5-8\]% Mana Stolen per Hit |
| +20 to Dexterity | +20 to Dexterity |
| +20 to Energy | +20 to Energy |
| +20% Enhanced Defense | Removed |

- Lesser Fade has a 30 second duration and provides +2% all resist, 1% physical damage reduction, and ~3% curse duration reduction per level. Level 10 Lesser Fade grants +20% all res, +10% pdr, and 28% curse duration reduction. Lesser Fade does _not_ stack with [Fade](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Fade "Fade") or [Burst of Speed](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Burst_of_Speed "Burst of Speed"), and will override them.

| +\[10-15\] to Vitality |

# Common Sets

## Common Sets

Set bonuses are listed separately rather than cumulatively - if multiple bonuses add the same attributes, those bonuses will be added together before taking effect.

Set items may be ethereal. They may also be [upgraded](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Recipes#Upgrading_Recipes "Recipes"). Unless upgraded, common sets only include normal bases.

In addition to the changes listed here, all melee weapons also gain Melee Attacks Deal Splash Damage.

[![](https://static.wikitide.net/projectdiablo2wiki/c/cf/Infernal_Cranium.png)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/File:Infernal_Cranium.png)

**Cap**

- **Base Defense:** 3-5

- **Base Durability:** 16


**Defense:** 3-5

**Defense (2 Items):** 7-401 (was 5-203)

**Required Level:** 3

**Minimum Item Level:** 7

**Occurrence Rate:** 7/10

| Before | After |
| --- | --- |
| All Resistances +10 | All Resistances +10 |
| 20% Damage Taken Gained as Mana when Hit | 20% Damage Taken Gained as Mana when Hit |
| +\[2-198\] Defense (+2 per Character Level) (2 Items) | +\[4-396\] Defense (+4 per Character Level) (2 Items) |

[![](https://static.wikitide.net/projectdiablo2wiki/a/a9/Infernal_Sign.png)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/File:Infernal_Sign.png)

**Heavy Belt**

- **Base Defense:** 6

- **Base Durability:** 18

- **Base Potion Rows:** 3


**Defense:** 31

**Required Strength:** 45

**Required Level:** 5

**Minimum Item Level:** 7

**Occurrence Rate:** 7/14

| Before | After |
| --- | --- |
| +25 Defense | +25 Defense |
| +20 to Life | +20 to Life |
| Poison Resist +25% (2 Items) | Poison Resist +45%(2 Items) |
| Half Freeze Duration (Complete Set) | Cannot Be Frozen(Complete Set) |

#### Infernal Spire (Infernal Torch)

[![](https://static.wikitide.net/projectdiablo2wiki/a/aa/Dagger_D2.png)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/File:Dagger_D2.png)

**Dagger** (was Grim Wand)

- **Base Damage:** 1 to 4 (Grim Wand was 5 to 11)

- **Base Durability:** 32 (Grim Wand was 15)

- **Base Speed Modifier:**-20 (Grim Wand was 10)

- **Base Melee Range:** 1 (Grim Wand was 0)

- **Base Maximum Sockets:** 1 (2 for upgraded versions)


**One-Hand Damage:** 9 to 10, Avg 9.5 (Grim Wand was 13 to 14, Avg 13.5)

**Required Level:** 5

| Before | After |
| --- | --- |
| +1 to Necromancer Skills | +1 to Necromancer Skills |
| +8 to Minimum Damage | +8 to Minimum Damage |
| +150% Damage to Undead | +150% Damage to Undead |
|  | 20% Deadly Strike |
| +\[10-990\] to Attack Rating (+10 per Character Level) (2 Items) | +\[10-990\] to Attack Rating (+10 per Character Level) (2 Items) |
| +\[3-297\] to Mana (+3 per Character Level) (Complete Set) | +2 to [Poison Strike](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Poison_Strike "Poison Strike")(Complete Set) |

| Before | After |
| --- | --- |

|  | +3 to Mana after each Kill (2 Items) |

# Uncommon Sets

## Uncommon Sets

Set bonuses are listed separately rather than cumulatively - if multiple bonuses add the same attributes, those bonuses will be added together before taking effect.

Set items may be ethereal. They may also be [upgraded](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Recipes#Upgrading_Recipes "Recipes").

In addition to the changes listed here, all melee weapons also gain Melee Attacks Deal Splash Damage.

# Class-Focused Sets

## Class-Focused Sets

Set bonuses are listed separately rather than cumulatively - if multiple bonuses add the same attributes, those bonuses will be added together before taking effect.

Set items may be ethereal. They may also be [upgraded](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Recipes#Upgrading_Recipes "Recipes").

In addition to the changes listed here, all melee weapons also gain Melee Attacks Deal Splash Damage.

# Runeword Helms

Runewords can only be made in regular items (ethereal or non-ethereal), and the socket count must be exact. They _cannot_ be made in items whose rarity is magic or higher.

Runeword changes include [rune](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Runes "Runes") changes.

- Blink is the same as [Teleport](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Teleport "Teleport"), except it costs no mana and doesn't temporarily reduce spell damage.

# Runeword Shields

## Shield Runewords

Runewords can only be made in regular items (ethereal or non-ethereal), and the socket count must be exact. They _cannot_ be made in items whose rarity is magic or higher.

Runeword changes include [rune](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Runes "Runes") changes.

### Ancient's Pledge

**3-Socket Shields**

**Ral  Ort  Tal**

**Required Level:** 21

| Before | After |
| --- | --- |
| +50% Enhanced Defense | +50% Enhanced Defense |
| Cold Resist +43% | Cold Resist +43% |
| Lightning Resist +48% | Lightning Resist +48% |
| Fire Resist +48% | Fire Resist +48% |
| Poison Resist +48% | Poison Resist +48% |
| 10% Damage Taken Gained as Mana when Hit | 10% Damage Taken Gained as Mana when Hit |

Ancient's Pledge is an introductory runeword and adds relatively little to the item beyond the +35% fire/lightning/poison resists gained from the runes themselves. Compare to 3 [perfect diamonds](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Gems "Gems"), which grants +57% to all resistances.

# Runeword Weapons

## Item Base Requirements

Runewords can only be made in regular items, and the socket count must be exact. They _cannot_ be made in items whose rarity is magic or higher.

Melee Weapons include all non-ranged weapons except Orbs. Technically, Wands are still classified as melee weapons despite their similarities to orbs and lack of melee splash damage.

Note that the in-game tooltips can sometimes be misleading since they refer to weapon "super-types" rather than the "sub-types" that are relevant in most scenarios.

- Wands/Orbs are _not_ part of the Staff sub-type

- Scepters are _not_ part of the (Tipped) Mace sub-type
- Clubs, Tipped Maces, and Hammers are all commonly referred to as Maces, but Clubs/Hammers are _not_ part of the (Tipped) Mace sub-type. To help differentiate the Mace super-type and Mace sub-type, the latter is called "Tipped Maces" instead.

  - Clubs:
    - Club, Cudgel, Truncheon
    - Spiked Club, Barbed Club, Tyrant Club
  - Tipped Maces:
    - Mace, Flanged Mace, Reinforced Mace
    - Morning Star, Jagged Star, Devil Star
    - Flail, Knout, Scourge
  - Hammers:
    - War Hammer, Battle Hammer, Legendary Mallet
    - Maul, War Club, Ogre Maul
    - Great Maul, Martel de Fer, Thunder Maul

## General Changes

- Many weapon runewords can be made in additional bases:
  - All runewords that can be made in Polearms can now also be made in Spears ( [Crescent Moon](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Crescent_Moon "RWWeapons"), [Insight](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Insight "RWWeapons"), [Obedience](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Obedience "RWWeapons"), [Rift](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Rift "RWWeapons"), [Infinity](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Infinity "RWWeapons"), [Destruction](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Destruction "RWWeapons"), [Doom](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Doom "RWWeapons"), [Pride](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Pride "RWWeapons"))
  - Staves can now also be used to make: [Spirit](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Spirit "RWWeapons"), [Beast](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Beast "RWWeapons"), [Infinity](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Infinity "RWWeapons"), [Destruction](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Destruction "RWWeapons"), [Last Wish](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Last_Wish "RWWeapons"), [Doom](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Doom "RWWeapons"), [Pride](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Pride "RWWeapons")
  - Claws can now also be used to make: [Steel](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Steel "RWWeapons"), [King's Grace](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#King's_Grace "RWWeapons"), [Black](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Black "RWWeapons"), [Lawbringer](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Lawbringer "RWWeapons"), [Crescent Moon](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Crescent_Moon "RWWeapons")
  - [Famine](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Famine "RWWeapons") can be made in Swords (in addition to Axes/Hammers)
  - [Rift](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Rift "RWWeapons") can be made in Swords (in addition to Scepters/Polearms and now Spears)
  - [Doom](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Doom "RWWeapons") can be made in Swords/Scepters (in addition to Axes/Hammers/Polearms and now Spears/Staves)
  - [Insight](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Insight "RWWeapons") can be made in Scepters (in addition to Staves/Polearms and now Spears)
  - [Voice of Reason](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Voice_of_Reason "RWWeapons") can be made in Bows/Crossbows (in addition to Swords/Tipped Maces)
  - [Obedience](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Obedience "RWWeapons") can be made in Hammers (in addition to Polearms and now Spears)
- Added new runewords:
  - [Pattern](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Pattern "RWWeapons") (was present in vanilla, but disabled)
  - [Plague](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Plague "RWWeapons") (was present in vanilla, but disabled)
  - [Neophyte](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Neophyte "RWWeapons")
  - [Rampage](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Rampage "RWWeapons")
  - [Dominion](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Dominion "RWWeapons")
  - [Zenith](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Zenith "RWWeapons")
  - [Unbending Will](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Unbending_Will "RWWeapons") (from D2 Resurrected)
  - [Mist](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Mist "RWWeapons") (from D2 Resurrected)
  - [Obsession](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Obsession "RWWeapons") (from D2 Resurrected)
  - [Asylum](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/RWWeapons#Asylum "RWWeapons")
- Runeword changes include [rune](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Runes "Runes") changes

| Adds 3-14 Cold Damage |
| 7% Life Stolen per Hit |

- WARNING: Prayer will be cast continuously, spending about 3.5 mana/second to maintain itself. Make sure you have adequate sources of mana regen if you wish to use this runeword on your playable character.

# Runes and Gems

## Runes

All runes are now stackable. Runes can be switched between their _stacked_ and _unstacked_ forms with [shortcuts](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/General_Changes#Quality-of-Life "General Changes"), and can only be placed in items when in their _unstacked_ form.

For rune effects that have been changed, changes are shown in blue with the original effects shown in gray.

| 33 | [![](https://static.wikitide.net/projectdiablo2wiki/1/1c/RuneZod.png)](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/File:RuneZod.png) | **Zod** | 69 | Indestructible | Indestructible | Indestructible | High |

The term "high rune" refers to any rune that cannot drop from the Hellforge quest, which is Vex or higher. It is not to be confused with the troublesomely-named "HR" unit of currency, which can be used with any sufficiently-valuable item rather than just high runes.

High runes typically form the core of market trading currencies due to their rarity and general usefulness, while upper "mid runes" (Lem through Gul) are close enough in value to be traded in a similar fashion, especially during the beginning of each ladder season. Below Lem, rune values are too low for individual runes to be practically referred to in terms of HRs, and are traded more often in bulk rather than as individual tokens of currency. Beyond runes, few items are used as ubiquitously as currency, with the most notable exception being [Worldstone Shards](https://wiki.projectdiablo2.com/wiki/Worldstone_Shard "Worldstone Shard").

## Gems

Flawless and Perfect gems are now stackable. Flawless gems now begin dropping in Act 4 Normal, and Perfect gems can now drop in Hell.

Gem effects have not been changed from vanilla D2, but are included here for convenience.
